<Name>Mrs Mom< /Name><date>1449052753335</date><Rate>1</Rate><Review>NOT PROFESSIONAL QUALITY IMAGES. BELOW AVERAGE, and cell phones yield far better images. It is all about whether the photographer understands their settings. I never thought I would say that Lifetouch takes wonderful school pictures, until my daughter's school switched to Studio 1 last year.  The images are consistently bad quality, not even remotely professional.  Last year, besides having an unpleasantly bright face from what appears to be on-camera flash, the camera lens' focus was on my daughter's shirt, so her eyes were a bit blurry.  We had her retake, and the retake was not great, but better than blurred eyes.  This year, the flash on her face was even brighter, and when retakes were done, her face was even more unusually and unpleasantly brighter than the last image (and her hair wasn't looked into by the photographer).  Any company offering professional photography services should know that a  simple inexpensive diffuser is needed to make the flash emit more natural and appealing results, instead of an unusually bright face.  Or a proper lighting set-up would do the job.  Studio 1 apparently is just a business that takes pictures, but is not knowledgeable of the fundamentals of photography and lighting.  Very disappointed.  I was looking forward to her school pictures, but it's such a waste of money that I would rather take my own pictures of her.< /Review>< Pics>

I ordered catering for 16 people. I ordered about 1 hr and  45 mins before I needed it and they were able to accommodate it. The food was ready by the time I got there (I was late by 15 mins)  so that was a relief since I was running late.  I didn't know they deliver for just $5, so I think that is a great value for the service. Might use their delivery in the future.

The food I ordered was correct and complete.  They provided the napkins, utensils and plates... everything was there as I requested.  The food was still hot,  it didn't disappoint.
I was happy with the whole experience and purchase. Very fast and convenient.< /review>

< review>
Really gave me an Ellis Island vibe inside with a sand colored polished brick on the walls and darker vintage lights on the ceiling. There were so many shops but the coolest part was being able to walk outside and up onto the bridge like dock and look at the golden gate or even back at the Port of San Francisco signage.

Really cool place - didn't end up buying or eating anything but it was worth following through on the recommendation to see it!<//review>

The Laguna Niguel Farmers Market has a very good blend of farm grown produce and fruit as well as healthy alternative products. You can buy fresh bread there, grass-fed beef and even fish. But the best part of the market is the avocado oil vendor, AVO-CO... they sell California grown avocado oil and flavored balsamic vinegars. They alone make this Market worth visiting!</Text>

1520969326406< /Date>
< Text>
Great little market.

Plenty of parking and it's not too busy, so you can usually get what you need easily.

There is an awesome selection of vendors too:

Coffee, fruits, vegetables, nuts, yogurts, breads, juices, essential oils, pastries, tamales, soups, seasonings, flowers, succulents, eggs, kombucha, everything!

Starts at 8 am and shuts down at noon, so it is a great way to kick off your Sunday.</Text>

< review>
The office is not easily seen from Gonzales Street.  You need to drive into the strip mall's parking lot in order to find the office.  Once you find it, across from Wells Fargo Bank, you can see the sign, Oxnard Dentistry, posted high up.  The interior is clean and modern, and the front office staff is very pleasant.  A real joy, compared to some other offices I have visited.  I had to wait much longer past my scheduled appointment time to receive my teeth cleaning, but it could be explained by the fact it was my first visit.  I met Dr. Keihani, who is quite pleasant and gentle.  A real pleasure.  His assistant then cleaned my teeth.  She explained the procedures she used so that I can gain a better understanding of what she was doing.  Dr. Keihani and the assistant recommended additional products and services, but there was no pressure placed on me to purchase them.  Overall, I am rating this service with five stars.  I plan to return in the future.<//review>

Sedation Dentistry
What is sedation dentistry?
Sedation dentistry refers to a relaxation technique that alleviates stress in patients who experience significant anxiety during dental procedures.

In most cases, sedation dentistry offers anesthetic to help you get through a procedure. However, sedation dentistry doesnâ€™t involve general anesthesia. Still, Dr. Keihani and his team offer multiple levels of sedation to make you as comfortable as possible.

The teamâ€™s compassionate approach to sedation dentistry is focused on making sure you never avoid dental procedures because of dental anxiety.

What are the different levels of sedation dentistry?
There are various levels of sedation dentistry. The three primary ones include:

Nitrous oxide inhalation sedation (laughing gas)
As the most common type of sedation, nitrous oxide inhalation sedation refers to a procedure during which Dr. Keihani places a mask over your nose. You breathe in nitrous oxide throughout the procedure, allowing you to relax. Itâ€™s most recommended for children and young adults, as the effects of nitrous oxide subside within hours of your dental procedure, allowing you to resume your daily activities.

< Review>
Walked in as a new patient.  Promptly helped by the team at the reception desk and enrolled.  They got me in the same day even though it was busy.

Dentist took a look and gave me a detailed plan going forward.

Excellent staff, friendly and attentive including the dental assistants and administrative staff.  I can see why the ratings are so high.

The wallpaper in the medical rooms is a tropical beach scene with white sand and crystal clear  blue water which faces the patient in the dental chair.  It might sound gimmicky but it's actually extremely soothing and comforting as many people have anxiety and fear at the dentist office.  Very nice touch.

Brent Minick</Review>
